~\newline
 One should never execute the source code which is being analyzed. ~\newline
~\newline
 However, for testing purposes it can be useful to see if one\textquotesingle{}s logic for parsing expressions evaluates properly. And so, for testing only, the \doxylink{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_interfaces_1_1_i_evaluator}{IEvaluator} exists. ~\newline

 Again, the ILuth\+Compiler\+Service should NEVER execute source code which it is analyzing. Only perform static analysis of source code }{\pageref{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_interfaces_1_1_i_evaluator}}{}

\item\contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_i_text_editor_edit_context}{Luthetus.\+Text\+Editor.\+Razor\+Lib.\+Text\+Editors.\+Models.\+IText\+Editor\+Edit\+Context}} \\*If one invokes, "{}\+\_\+ = edit\+Context.\+Get\+View\+Model\+Modifier(view\+Model\+Key);"{}.~\newline
 Then a side effect occurs where the view model with the provided view\+Model\+Key, will be marked as a having been modified.~\newline
 After a Post is finished, the text editor service iterates over all \textquotesingle{}modified\textquotesingle{} view models and re-\/renders them.~\newline
 This behavior is a bit hacky since it requires some amount of \textquotesingle{}hidden knowledge\textquotesingle{}.~\newline
 To get a view model without marking it as modified, use the optional parameter, \textquotesingle{}is\+Readonly\textquotesingle{} and set it to \textquotesingle{}true\textquotesingle{}.~\newline
 The main reason for making this comment, is that I sometimes assign the result of \textquotesingle{}Get\+View\+Model\+Modifier\textquotesingle{} to discard.~\newline
 When I do this it feels especially hacky, so I want to leave a paper trail of what I mean by that statement.~\newline
 }{\pageref{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_i_text_editor_edit_context}}{}

\item\contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_i_text_editor_model}{Luthetus.\+Text\+Editor.\+Razor\+Lib.\+Text\+Editors.\+Models.\+IText\+Editor\+Model}} \\*Stores the \doxylink{struct_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_characters_1_1_models_1_1_rich_character}{Rich\+Character} class instances that represent the text.~\newline
~\newline
 Each \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_text_editor_model}{Text\+Editor\+Model} has a unique underlying resource uri.~\newline
~\newline
 Therefore, if one has a text file named "{}my\+Homework.\+txt"{}, then only one \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_text_editor_model}{Text\+Editor\+Model} can exist with the resource uri of "{}my\+Homework.\+txt"{}.~\newline

\item\contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_symbols_1_1_on_click_symbol}{Luthetus.\+Text\+Editor.\+Razor\+Lib.\+Compiler\+Services.\+Syntax.\+Symbols.\+On\+Click\+Symbol}} \\*TODO\+: This type should be changed. It is being made to permit simple \textquotesingle{}onclick\textquotesingle{} markers... ...but its not quite a \textquotesingle{}Symbol\textquotesingle{}. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} Just happens to be the case that a symbol can act as a marker for some "{}event like thing"{} so it works to have it here for now. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} The main issue is that the Symbol instances will apply syntax highlighting. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} For this \textquotesingle{}\doxylink{struct_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_symbols_1_1_on_click_symbol}{On\+Click\+Symbol}\textquotesingle{} we would preferably not apply any syntax highlighting. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} For example\+: "{}cd .."{} I want to syntax highlight \textquotesingle{}cd\textquotesingle{} as the target file path, but NOT syntax highlight the arguments \textquotesingle{}..\textquotesingle{} \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} If I use a symbol to syntax highlight \textquotesingle{}cd\textquotesingle{}, then it might be overridden by the \textquotesingle{}\doxylink{struct_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_symbols_1_1_on_click_symbol}{On\+Click\+Symbol}\textquotesingle{} of which is not supposed to alter the syntax highlighting. (it depends on the order that the symbols are applied) }{\pageref{struct_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_symbols_1_1_on_click_symbol}}{}

As of this comment, \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_text_editor_model}{Text\+Editor\+Model} is a class which is frequently re-\/constructed with new(). A Cancellation\+Token\+Source as a property would therefore not work. One would Cancel() then new() up another Cancellation\+Token\+Source and update the property. Yet its possible that instance of \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_text_editor_model}{Text\+Editor\+Model} isn\textquotesingle{}t even being used anymore by that point. So a readonly object wrapper which then contains the Cancellation\+Token\+Source ensures it doesn\textquotesingle{}t get lost }{\pageref{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_internals_1_1_save_file_helper}}{}

\\*TODO\+: Decide on what folder this class belongs in... ...I\textquotesingle{}m working on the Quick Actions / Refactor context menu (2024-\/08-\/16) and the issue is that, the context menu is populated with menu options from within the \doxylink{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_text_editors_1_1_models_1_1_i_text_editor_edit_context}{IText\+Editor\+Edit\+Context}. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} But by the time the user picks a context menu option, the text editor may have been edited, thus invalidating any stored Func$<$\+Task$>$ that is given for a menu option\textquotesingle{}s onclick. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} So, each menu option needs to make a separate Post to the \doxylink{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_i_text_editor_service}{IText\+Editor\+Service} upon onclick. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} But, all of the variables that were created to construct the menu options, during the old post, are still within scope when typing out code for the menu option\textquotesingle{}s onclick if written inline as a lambda function. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} So, most importantly this class exists to avoid accidental usage of old text editor state due to the variables being in scope. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} But this also probably is nice for readability, and re-\/usability of the refactor itself. \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} I don\textquotesingle{}t want a separate function within \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_commands_1_1_models_1_1_defaults_1_1_text_editor_command_default_functions}{Text\+Editor\+Command\+Default\+Functions} because it is a nice separation of concern to keep compiler service refactors in a separate file ~\newline
 The \doxylink{namespace_luthetus_1_1_common_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_tree_views}{Tree\+Views} were designed with a root consisting of 1 node. To get around this \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_common_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_tree_views_1_1_models_1_1_tree_view_adhoc}{Tree\+View\+Adhoc} can be used to have that top level root node be invisible to the user }{\pageref{class_luthetus_1_1_common_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_tree_views_1_1_models_1_1_tree_view_adhoc}}{}
